commit fc2dafae31feff74b82f4b31749e05534079c866
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Wed Oct 14 16:58:03 2015 +0800

    uboot2014: add dragonboard handler.
    
    sdmmc:For dragon board test, boot from sdc0 firstly, then try sdc2 at uboot. If sdc2 is invalid(not emmc/sd),
    modify device tree to disable sdc2. Because boot from sdc0, there is no valid timing parameters for sdc2
    in boot0's header. Updating timing parameters from boot0's header is wrong.
    Therefore, change sdc2's "sdc_ex_dly_used" in device tree to 0 to cancel updateing timing parameters.
    It is also necessary to delete flowing items from device tree to keep emmc working at hssdr mode:
    	mmc-ddr-1_8v           =
    	mmc-hs200-1_8v         =
    	mmc-hs400-1_8v         =
    	max-frequency          = 150000000
    The aim of dragon board test is only to check electrical connection.
    
    Signed-off-by: wangwei <wangwei@allwinnertech.com>

commit 2c018c17eed1572093c19e6e3f235d7583a3e3e2
Author: Vikram Kanigiri <vikram.kanigiri@arm.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 30 15:27:02 2015 +0800

    Initialise cpu ops after enabling data cache
    
    The cpu-ops pointer was initialized before enabling the data cache in the cold
    and warm boot paths. This required a DCIVAC cache maintenance operation to
    invalidate any stale cache lines resident in other cpus.
    
    This patch moves this initialization to the bl31_arch_setup() function
    which is always called after the data cache and MMU has been enabled.
    
    This change removes the need:
     1. for the DCIVAC cache maintenance operation.
     2. to initialise the CPU ops upon resumption from a PSCI CPU_SUSPEND
        call since memory contents are always preserved in this case.
    
    Change-Id: Ibb2fa2f7460d1a1f1e721242025e382734c204c6
    
    Signed-off-by: wangwei <wangwei@allwinnertech.com>

commit fbb5f65e786b1fa9b8974fb66f139774148f6be0
Author: Soby Mathew <soby.mathew@arm.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 30 15:27:01 2015 +0800

    Invalidate the dcache after initializing cpu-ops
    
    This patch fixes a crash due to corruption of cpu_ops
    data structure. During the secondary CPU boot, after the
    cpu_ops has been initialized in the per cpu-data, the
    dcache lines need to invalidated so that the update in
    memory can be seen later on when the dcaches are turned ON.
    Also, after initializing the psci per cpu data, the dcache
    lines are flushed so that they are written back to memory
    and dirty dcache lines are avoided.
    
    Fixes ARM-Software/tf-issues#271
    
    Change-Id: Ia90f55e9882690ead61226eea5a5a9146d35f313
    
    Signed-off-by: wangwei <wangwei@allwinnertech.com>

commit fc316e8d802b8b74fbed4c94c1416043cc1a7681
Author: Sandrine Bailleux <sandrine.bailleux@arm.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 30 15:27:00 2015 +0800

    Prevent optimisation of sysregs accessors calls
    
    Calls to system register read accessors functions may be optimised
    out by the compiler if called twice in a row for the same register.
    This is because the compiler is not aware that the result from
    the instruction may be modified by external agents. Therefore, if
    nothing modifies the register between the 2 reads as far as the
    compiler knows then it might consider that it is useless to read
    it twice and emit only 1 call.
    
    This behaviour is faulty for registers that may not have the same
    value if read twice in succession. E.g.: counters, timer
    control/countdown registers, GICv3 interrupt status registers and
    so on.
    
    The same problem happens for calls to system register write
    accessors functions. The compiler might optimise out some calls
    if it considers that it will produce the same result. Again, this
    behaviour is faulty for cases where intermediate writes to these
    registers make a difference in the system.
    
    This patch fixes the problem by making these assembly register
    accesses volatile.
    
    Fixes ARM-software/tf-issues#273
    
    Change-Id: I33903bc4cc4eea8a8d87bc2c757909fbb0138925
    
    Signed-off-by: wangwei <wangwei@allwinnertech.com>

commit 7ab5fc856dac1b41e3199f3827d06d563e7de4c2
Author: Achin Gupta <achin.gupta@arm.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 10 11:50:30 2014 +0000

    Precede a 'sev' with a 'dsb' in bakery lock code
    
    This patch fixes a bug in the bakery lock implementation where a data
    synchronisation barrier instruction is not issued before sending an event as
    mandated by the ARMv8 ARM. This can cause a event to be signalled before the
    related memory accesses have completed resulting in erroneous execution.
    
    Fixes ARM-software/tf-issues#272
    
    Change-Id: I5ce02bf70afb001d967b9fa4c3f77442931d5349
    
    Signed-off-by: superm <superm@allwinnertech.com>

commit 2bee9d5bdf5166d1e80f155f562d890c9b606a16
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Tue Mar 24 13:35:08 2015 +0800

    mmc:sun50i: fix emmc's write/read frequency to 100MHz to be compatile perf1 and perf2.
    
    1. the emmc's max frequency of perf1 and perf2 are different. 100MHz can be supported by perf1 and perf2.
    2. the max frqunency of 3.0V io voltage is only 50MHz. In order to support to 100MHz, we must set io
    voltage to 1.8V by on/off some resistors on PCB board, and add "sdc_io_1v8 = 1" to [card2_boot_para] in sys_config.fex.

commit 8d1bbf3e11f1a4fbbcfbbef5cbde9d216f388dba
Author: Sugar <shuge@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Thu Nov 20 15:26:28 2014 +0800

    net: support hardware checksum function
    
    Uboot just use IP TCP/UDP protocols, it will calculate
    the checksum of packet by calling Netchecksum.
    
    But some MAC controller support hardware checksum, it will
    improve the checksum process. So add CONFIG_HARD_CHECKSUM
    to open hardware checksum.

    sd-mmc:sun9i:sunxi-dev: reduce the probablity of read uboot error during boot0 period.
    
    there two type of error during boot0 period:
    (1) initialize controller error;
    (2) read data error.
    we don't find the primary reason, but we make two modifications to reduce these two errors:
    (1) change the initial status of gpio-f before initializing controller;
    (2) change the bias voltage of gpio-f to 3.0V;

commit ed6babb129ae389b2418788fb323ba0633673768
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Sat Dec 7 17:52:05 2013 +0800

    nand, sun8iw3: fix up scanning timing parameters error.
    
    scanning timing parameters is based on the data in block 4. if block 4 is
    a bad block, we'll get wrong timing parameters.
    now, we read and check data from block 2 to block 10 firstly, select valid
    data in the first good block. the next scanning is based on this valid data.

commit b053c93f1cca1c4c5c6827e347633cd90db7b8ca
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Sat Dec 7 12:48:49 2013 +0800

    nand, sun8iw3: support micron 20nm L85A and 16nm L95B new nand.

commit bbdae39ba16b14afacc79f30de122b7c9ed9ec8f
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Fri Dec 6 22:03:12 2013 +0800

    nand, sun8iw3: support to change nand access frequency and two-plane architecture from external script sys_config.fex.
    
    1. support to change nand access frequency from external script sys_config.fex. it is convenient to
    debug some down-grade nand without update binary libnand.
    2. support to use old multi-plane architecture. during physical layer initialization, the driver
    search old physical layer parameters from block 12 on chip 0. if get valid parameters, it will use
    the old multi-plane architecure. if get invalid parameters or get failed, it will use single plane
    architecture.
    these physical parameters are updated when all chips are erased during update firmware, and written
    to the first good block after block 12 in chip 0. now, it supports to change multi-plane architecture
    through script sys_config.fex instead of modifing binary libnand.
    by the way, the multi-plane operation can amplify the logic page as two physical page and is very
    good to seqential write speed.

commit 47947f1a32f63f3936b0c2c43efc584825f2982c
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Fri Dec 6 20:19:28 2013 +0800

    nand:sun8iw3: fix bug in the exit flow of hynix 20nm LSB mode.
    
    there is a bug in the exit flow of hyinx 20nm LSB mode. it is that we don't wait rb signal ready after the last
    dummy read operation. this bug may cause massive ecc error after OTA updates boot0. it is found on A31 platform firstly.
    
    Conflicts:
    
    	u-boot-2011.09/nand_sunxi/sun8iw3/libnand-sun8iw3

commit b71c2a4e877c21c434b7fa23c38d72cf8c6f0437
Author: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
Date:   Sat Nov 30 18:40:45 2013 +0800

    nand, sun8iw3: fix bug in the flow of super resume.
    
    1. during super resume, before scan edo and delay-chain for sdr/ddr interface, initialize
    edo(=1) for sdr and nvddr interface at 10MHz, or edo(=2) and delay-chain(=0x1f) for toggle
    ddr interface at 20MHZ.
    2. change access frequency of TC58TEG6DCJTA00 from 40MHz to 30MHz.
    3. to improve the accuracy of scanning result of timing parameters, read 4KB~8KB data instead
    of 1KB.
    
    Signed-off-by: wenjiaqiang <wenjiaqiang@allwinnertech.com>
